routines to finish before shutting down audit backend.\n79: \twg sync.WaitGroup\n80: \n81: \t// Limits the number of batches sent to the delegate backend per second.\n82: \tthrottle interconnected components that create, evaluate, process, and dispatch audit events:\\n\\n## Audit Event Creation and Context Management\\nThe audit logging flow begins with initialization and context management. The `WithAuditInit` filter in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit_init.go` initializes the audit context for each request, generating or extracting an Audit-ID from the request header. This is paired with `WithAuditContext` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/context.go`, which creates the core `AuditContext` structure that holds the audit event being captured and the evaluated policy configuration.\\n\\nThe `AuditContext` is stored in the request context and provides thread-safe access to audit annotations via `AddAuditAnnotation` and related methods. The `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/request.go` file contains critical functions for populating audit events: `LogRequestMetadata` captures HTTP request information (URI, user, source IPs, verb), `LogRequestObject` serializes the request body, and `LogResponseObject` captures response data.\\n\\n## Audit Policy Evaluation\\nThe audit policy evaluation component in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/checker.go` implements the `PolicyRuleEvaluator` interface (defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/evaluator.go`). The `NewPolicyRuleEvaluator` function creates an evaluator from a policy loaded by `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/policy/reader.go`, which parses audit policy YAML/JSON files. The `EvaluatePolicyRule` method matches incoming requests against policy rules by checking users, groups, verbs, namespaces, resources, and non-resource URLs, returning a `RequestAuditConfig` that specifies the audit level, omit stages, and whether to omit managed fields.\\n\\n## Audit Event Processing and Dispatch\\nThe core request handler decorator `WithAudit` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/audit.go` orchestrates the full audit flow. It calls `evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent` to evaluate the policy and create the initial audit event, then uses `processAuditEvent` to send events to the audit sink at different request stages (RequestReceived, ResponseStarted, ResponseComplete, and Panic). The function tracks response status codes and latencies through an `auditResponseWriter` decorator that implements HTTP response writer interception.\\n\\n## Audit Backend Architecture\\nAudit events flow through a dispatch system defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/union.go`. The `Union` function creates a composite backend that sends events to multiple backends in sequence. Three main backend implementations are provided:\\n\\n1. **File Logging Backend** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/log/backend.go`): The `NewBackend` function creates a file-based backend that writes audit events in JSON or legacy text format to an I/O writer (typically a rotating file via lumberjack).\\n\\n2. **Webhook Backend** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/webhook/webhook.go`): The `NewBackend` function creates an HTTP webhook backend that batches events and sends them to an external service via POST requests. It implements exponential backoff retry logic for resilience.\\n\\n3. **Buffered/Batching Backend** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/buffered/buffered.go`): The `NewBackend` function wraps a delegate backend to batch events asynchronously. It supports configurable buffer sizes, batch sizes, batching intervals, and throttling (QPS-based rate limiting) for controlling the flow of events to the delegate backend.\\n\\n## Audit Event Truncation\\nThe truncate backend in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/audit/truncate/truncate.go` handles truncation of large request and response bodies.
